        The xml files are now divided according to the internal naming of the sections,
        Śālākyatantra (adhyāyas 1-26), Kumāratantra (27-38), Kāyacikitsātantra (39-59),
        Bhūtavidyātantra (60-62), Tantrabhūṣaṇādhyāya (63-66).</change>

      <div n="6" type="sthāna">


        <head xml:lang="en">[Uttaratantra 39-24-57 Kāyacikitsātantra]</head>

        <note xml:lang="en">The Nepalese MSS do not follow the sequence of the vulgate here. The
          Nepalese edition should follow the Nepalese MSS, i.e., vulgate 6.38 is followed by
          6.60</note>

        <div n="39" type="adhyāya">
          <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 39, Kāyacikitsā 1 : draft edition based on MS K]</head>

          <note xml:lang="en">[This adhyāya is currently a rough version based on MSS NAK 5-333 and
            699, being edited (2023-10-04).]</note>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.1">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.39.1</label>
            <caesura/>
             athāto jvarapratiṣedhaṃ adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||<anchor n="SS.6.39.1-n1"/>
          </l>

          <ab corresp="#SS.6.39.1" type="apparatus">
            <list type="Note">
              <item xml:lang="en" corresp="#SS.6.39.1-n1">In reading <foreign>-utpatti</foreign>,
                the scribe of H may have been influenced by the title <foreign>grahotpatti</foreign>
                of the immediately preceding adhyāya in his manuscript (he omits the
                  <foreign>yonivyāpat</foreign> adhyāya).</item>
            </list>
          </ab>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.2"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.3.add">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.39.3.add</label>
            <caesura/>
             atha khalu vatsasuśruta </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.3">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.39.3</label>
            <caesura/>
             yenāmṛtam apāṃ madhyād uddhṛtaṃ pūrvvajanmani |
            <caesura/>
             yato 'maratvaṃ saṃprāptās tridaśās tridiveśvarāḥ ||<anchor n="SS.6.39.3-n1"/>
          </l>

          <ab corresp="#SS.6.39.3" type="apparatus">
            <list type="Note">
              <item xml:lang="en" corresp="#SS.6.39.3-n1">Dalhaṇa (p. 671) reported Jejjaṭa's
                reading <foreign>tridaśās tridaśeśvarāḥ</foreign>, which is a mixture of the
                readings of witnesses K and H.</item>
            </list>
          </ab>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.4">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.39.4</label>
            <caesura/>
             śiṣyās taṃ devam āsīnaṃ papracchuḥ suśrutādayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vraṇasyopadravāḥ proktā vraṇinām apy ataḥ paraṃ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.5">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.39.5</label>
            <caesura/>
             samāsato vyāsataś ca brūhi no bhiṣajām vara |
            <caesura/>
             upadraveṇa juṣṭasya vraṇaḥ kṛcchreṇa sidhyati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.6">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.39.6</label>
            <caesura/>
             upadravāś ca vraṇinaḥ kṛcchrasādhytamo mataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             prakṣīṇabalamāṃsasya śeṣadhātuparikṣayāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.7ab">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.39.7ab</label>
            <caesura/>
             tasmād upadravān kṛtsnān vadasva vadatām vara || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.7cd"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.8">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.39.8</label>
            <caesura/>
             teṣān tad vacanaṃ śrutvā prābravīd bhiṣajām varaḥ ||
            <caesura/>
             jvaram ādau pravakṣyāmi sa rogānīkarāṭ smṛtaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.9">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.39.9</label>
            <caesura/>
             rudrakopāgnisaṃbhūtaḥ sarvvabhūtapratāpanaḥ ||
            <caesura/>
             tais tair nnāmabhir anyeṣāṃ sattvānām parikīrttyate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.10">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.39.10</label>
            <caesura/>
             janmādau nidhane caiva bhavatīha na saṃśayaḥ ||
            <caesura/>
             ataḥ sarvavikārāṇāṃ jvaro rājā prakīrttitaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.11">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.39.11</label>
            <caesura/>
             ṛte devamanuṣyebhyo nānyo viṣahate tu taṃ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.12"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.13">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.39.13</label>
            <caesura/>
             svedāvarodhaḥ santāpaḥ sarvvāṅgagrahaṇam tathā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.14">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.39.14</label>
            <caesura/>
             yugapad yatra roge tu jvara ity upadiśyate ||
            <caesura/>
             doṣaiḥ pṛthak samastaiś ca dvandvair āgantur eva ca | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.15">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.39.15</label>
            <caesura/>
             anekakāraṇotpannaḥ smṛtas tv aṣṭavidho jvaraḥ ||
            <caesura/>
             doṣāḥ prakupitā gāḍham apathyāhārasevinaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.16">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.39.16</label>
            <caesura/>
             vyāpya deham aśeṣeṇa jvaram āpādayanti ha || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.17"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.18"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.19ab"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.19cd">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.39.19cd</label>
            <caesura/>
             adhimithyā<pc> </pc>prayuktaiś ca snehādyaiḥ karmmabhir nnṛṇāṃ |<anchor
              n="SS.6.39.19cd-n1"/>
          </l>

          <ab corresp="#SS.6.39.19cd" type="apparatus">
            <list type="Emendation">
              <item xml:lang="en" corresp="#SS.6.39.19cd-n1">Witnesses N and H read
                  <foreign>api-</foreign> for the emended reading <foreign>adhi-</foreign>. While
                both MSS seem to have read <foreign>pa</foreign>, it should be noted that in the
                script of MS K, <foreign>pa</foreign> and <foreign>dha</foreign> are somewhat
                similarly written. This suggests a reading <foreign>dha</foreign> that was misread
                early in the transmission.</item>
            </list>
          </ab>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.20">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.39.20</label>
            <caesura/>
             vividhād abhighātāc ca rogotthānāt prapākataḥ ||
            <caesura/>
             śramāt kṣayād ajīrṇṇāc ca viṣāt sātmyartuparyayāt | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.21">

             oṣadhīpuṣpagandhāc ca kokānnakṣatrapīḍayā ||
            <caesura/>
             abhiśāpābhicārābhyāṃ manobhūtābhiśaṅkayā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.22">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.39.22</label>
            <caesura/>
             strīṇām avaprajātānāṃ prajātānān tathāhitaiḥ ||
            <caesura/>
             stanyāvataṇe jvaro doṣaiḥ prakupyati | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.23">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.39.23</label>
            <caesura/>
             tair vvegavadbhir bbahudhā samudbhrāntai rvvimārggagaiḥ ||
            <caesura/>
             vikṣipyamāṇo 'ntaragnirbhbhavatyāśu bahiś caraḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.24">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.39.24</label>
            <caesura/>
             ruṇaddhi cāpy apān dhātuṃ yasmāt tasmāj jvarāturaḥ ||
            <caesura/>
             bhavaty atyuṣṇagātraś ca svidyatena ca sarvvaśaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.25">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.39.25</label>
            <caesura/>
             śramor atirvivarṇṇatvaṃ vairasyaṃ nayanaplavaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             icchādveṣau muhuś cāpi śītavātātapādiṣu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.26">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.39.26</label>
            <caesura/>
             jṛmbhāṅgamarddo gurutā romaharṣo 'rucis tamaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             apraharṣaś ca śīta ca bhavaty utpatsyati jvare || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.27">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.39.27</label>
            <caesura/>
             sāmānyato viśeṣāt tu jṛmbhāty arthan samīraṇāt |
            <caesura/>
             pittān nayanarddāhaḥ kaphād annārucis tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.28">

            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.29">

            <caesura/>
             vepathurvviṣamo vegaḥ kaṇṭhauṣṭhapariśoṣaṇaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             nidrānāśaḥ kṣayastaṃbho gātrāṇāṃ raukṣyam eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.30">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.39.30</label>
            <caesura/>
             śiroruggātra rugvaktraṃ vairasyaṃ gāḍhaviṭkatā |
            <caesura/>
             śūlādhmānau jṛmbhaṇañ ca bhavaty anilaje jvare || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.31">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.39.31</label>
            <caesura/>
             vegastīkṣṇomatisāraś ca mahādāho nidrālpaś ca tathā vamiḥ |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.20">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.43.20</label>
            <caesura/>
             sugandhibhiḥ śalavaṇair yogaiḥ sājājiśarkaraiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             viḍaṃgagāḍhaidhānyāmlaṃ pāyayed hitam uttamaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.21">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.43.21</label>
            <caesura/>
             hṛdisthitāḥ patantyeva madhastāt krimayo nṛṇāṃ |
            <caesura/>
             yavānnaṃ vitarec cāsmaisaviḍaṃgamataḥ param iti || kāyaci || kṛ || ||</l>

            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.57.14</label>
            <caesura/>
            kṣaudrāyutāni vitaren mukhadhāvanārthaṃm anyāni tiktakaṭukāni ca bheṣajāni |
            <caesura/>
            mustādirājaphalavargadaśāṃgasiddhaḥ kvāthair jayen madhuyutair vividhaiś ca lehaiḥ || </l>
          
          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.15">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.57.15</label>
            <caesura/>
            mūtrāsavair guḍakṛtaiś ca tathāpy ariṣṭaiḥ kṣārāsavaiś ca madhumādhavatulyagandhaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
            syād eṣa eva kaphavātaharo vidhiś ca | śātiṃ gate hutabhuji praśamāya tasya | </l>
          
          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.16">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.57.16</label>
            <caesura/>
            icchāvināśabhayajeṣu ca bādhakeṣu | bhāvād bhavāya vitaret khalu śalyatāpān |
            <caesura/>
            artheṣu cātipatiteṣu punarbhavāya paurāṇikaśrutimukhair avamānayeta iti || kāyaci || 20
            || 0 || </l>
          
          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.17">
            <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed. 6.57.17</label>
            <caesura/>
            cchardi hikkā śvāsakāsaḥ svaraghātam athāparaṃ |
            <caesura/>
            pratiśyāyaḥ krimiś caiva sodāvarttā visūcikā |
            <caesura/>
            arocakena ca tathā pūryate dvitīyo daśaḥ || ❈ ||</l>
